# Master Prompt Ledger

**Composition authority:** the extracted source PNG listed for each entry

Metadata below is normalized from `manifest.json`; prompt prose is preserved from the authored component ledgers.

## 1. `png/BIGPIC1/BIGPIC1_block_121_frame_000.png`

- Archive/block/frame: `BIGPIC1.DAX` / `121` / `0`
- Source size/ratio: `304×120` / `38:15`
- Category: `large_scene`
- Animated: `false`
- Authored in: `TITLE-BIGPIC-prompts.json`

### Prompt

Create a high-resolution photorealistic live-action fantasy reconstruction of the attached original Curse of the Azure Bonds image.

COMPOSITION LOCK — preserve exactly:
- source aspect ratio: 38:15;
- original camera angle, crop and horizon;
- major subject bounding boxes and their relative proportions;
- foreground/middle-ground/background allocation;
- count, placement, facing direction and scale of important people, creatures and objects;
- architecture, pathways, openings and major environmental shapes;
- negative space and panel readability.

SCENE CONTENT:
Reconstruct the wide, oblique overhead fantasy travel map as a physically built, photoreal relief-map landscape while retaining its map readability. The entire frame is continuous green terrain viewed from high above, with no sky and no human figures. A dominant rugged brown-gray mountain chain occupies roughly the left quarter and runs vertically; dark evergreen forest masses cluster across the center and lower half; thin blue rivers and dark winding roads thread between them. Keep the small settlement/fortified-location clusters, circular route nodes, and junctions in their original coordinates. Preserve the pale blue lake or coastal inlet in the upper-right corner and the exact balance of open grassland, woodland, mountains, water, and paths. Natural overcast daylight, restrained greens and earth tones, crisp terrain detail across the full depth.

COHESIVE GAME ART DIRECTION:
Grounded prestige live-action Forgotten Realms fantasy; realistic late-medieval materials and construction; natural skin, cloth, leather, wood, stone and metal; practical costumes and armor; physically coherent natural or motivated magical lighting; restrained cinematic color grading; subtle atmospheric depth; rich fine detail; serious dramatic tone. Match or exceed the realism and production quality of PIC1_block_080_village.png.

Do not add text, borders, logos, interface elements, modern objects, extra characters, extra limbs or unrelated fantasy decoration. Do not make it cartoon, anime, painterly, plastic, glossy, oversaturated, generic concept art or an obvious 3D render. Do not redesign the composition. The result must be immediately recognizable as the same scene at photographic realism.

IMAGE-SPECIFIC NEGATIVE/QUALITY CONSTRAINTS:
No eye-level horizon, clouds, labels, lettering, compass rose, decorative border, enlarged landmarks, added towns, armies, people, creatures, or invented monuments. Do not turn it into a flat parchment illustration or satellite image. Keep every route node and major terrain mass fixed; broad depth of field, no miniature tilt-shift blur.

Output one clean scene image with no frame or caption.

### Prompt

Create a high-resolution photorealistic live-action fantasy reconstruction of the attached original Curse of the Azure Bonds image.

COMPOSITION LOCK — preserve exactly:
- source aspect ratio: 38:15;
- original camera angle, crop and horizon;
- major subject bounding boxes and their relative proportions;
- foreground/middle-ground/background allocation;
- count, placement, facing direction and scale of important people, creatures and objects;
- architecture, pathways, openings and major environmental shapes;
- negative space and panel readability.

SCENE CONTENT:
Extreme close frontal portrait of one supernatural skull-faced demon filling the central third of an ultra-wide frame. Its pale bone face is centered, symmetrical and staring directly at camera with two small red glowing eyes, a triangular nasal cavity and a broad row of exposed teeth. Pointed ear or horn silhouettes extend sideways. A huge blue-white magical flame, mane, or crown rises above and behind the skull across most of the upper center. Exactly two large dark clawed hands enter from the far left and far right, curling inward to frame but not cover the face. The lower center burns with restrained red-orange fire and smoke while the outer background remains nearly black and deep blue. Hard motivated cyan light from above and ember light from below shape real bone, leathery claws, smoke and flame.

COHESIVE GAME ART DIRECTION:
Grounded prestige live-action Forgotten Realms fantasy; realistic late-medieval materials and construction; natural skin, cloth, leather, wood, stone and metal; practical costumes and armor; physically coherent natural or motivated magical lighting; restrained cinematic color grading; subtle atmospheric depth; rich fine detail; serious dramatic tone. Match or exceed the realism and production quality of PIC1_block_080_village.png.

Do not add text, borders, logos, interface elements, modern objects, extra characters, extra limbs or unrelated fantasy decoration. Do not make it cartoon, anime, painterly, plastic, glossy, oversaturated, generic concept art or an obvious 3D render. Do not redesign the composition. The result must be immediately recognizable as the same scene at photographic realism.

IMAGE-SPECIFIC NEGATIVE/QUALITY CONSTRAINTS:
One face and exactly two framing hands only. Do not add a torso, extra skulls, extra eyes, wings, jewelry, text, or scenery. Preserve the very wide negative space and edge-entering hand silhouettes. Do not reinterpret the blue crown as a solid hat or helmet; retain its ambiguous magical flame/aura character. Keep teeth and hand anatomy coherent, terrifying rather than comic, with controlled saturation and readable blacks.

Output one clean scene image with no frame or caption.

## 3. `png/BIGPIC2/BIGPIC2_block_120_frame_000.png`

- Archive/block/frame: `BIGPIC2.DAX` / `120` / `0`
- Source size/ratio: `304×120` / `38:15`

- Authored in: `TITLE-BIGPIC-prompts.json`

### Prompt

Create a high-resolution photorealistic live-action fantasy reconstruction of the attached original Curse of the Azure Bonds image.

COMPOSITION LOCK — preserve exactly:
- source aspect ratio: 38:15;
- original camera angle, crop and horizon;
- major subject bounding boxes and their relative proportions;
- foreground/middle-ground/background allocation;
- count, placement, facing direction and scale of important people, creatures and objects;
- architecture, pathways, openings and major environmental shapes;
- negative space and panel readability.

SCENE CONTENT:
Three disembodied villain heads float against a pure black sparse star field in a wide, shallow triangular cluster. Left head occupies approximately x18–46%, y19–89%: an angular gaunt human-like face in three-quarter view facing right, beneath a large sweeping pale-blue/deep-blue hood or headdress that arcs inward. Center head occupies approximately x39–62%, y31–93%: a medium-sized frontal woman positioned lower than both side heads, with a symmetrical face and an ornate circular red-violet headdress or hair mass dotted with small warm gold accents; tiny finger-like shapes may frame the lower chin exactly as in the source. Right head occupies approximately x58–86%, y18–90%: the widest and largest-by-mass creature or villain head, in three-quarter view facing left, with a prominent grin/jaw and a swept-back crest. A continuous restrained red-orange-violet magical arc spans approximately x26–78%, y5–31% above and behind the three heads. Preserve narrow black separation gaps between the faces, large empty black margins at both sides, and sparse tiny white stars. No bodies or ground plane.

COHESIVE GAME ART DIRECTION:
Grounded prestige live-action Forgotten Realms fantasy; realistic late-medieval materials and construction; natural skin, cloth, leather, wood, stone and metal; practical costumes and armor; physically coherent natural or motivated magical lighting; restrained cinematic color grading; subtle atmospheric depth; rich fine detail; serious dramatic tone. Match or exceed the realism and production quality of PIC1_block_080_village.png.

Do not add text, borders, logos, interface elements, modern objects, extra characters, extra limbs or unrelated fantasy decoration. Do not make it cartoon, anime, painterly, plastic, glossy, oversaturated, generic concept art or an obvious 3D render. Do not redesign the composition. The result must be immediately recognizable as the same scene at photographic realism.

IMAGE-SPECIFIC NEGATIVE/QUALITY CONSTRAINTS:
Exactly three heads, no fourth face. Keep the center woman lower and medium-sized; the right inward-facing head must remain the largest by mass, and the left inward-facing hood must preserve its long pale-blue arc. Do not pack the heads together or replace the black gaps with hair, robes, fog or nebula. No full bodies, shoulders, extra eyes, floating hands beyond the tiny source-implied shapes under the center chin, weapons, planets, architecture, elaborate clouds, text or border. Preserve the exact wide 38:15 crop, side margins, red halo extent and source bounding boxes. Avoid glamour styling, oversized horns, generic demons, merged anatomy or a dominant enlarged central portrait.

Output one clean scene image with no frame or caption.

- foreground/middle-ground/background allocation;
- count, placement, facing direction and scale of important people, creatures and objects;
- architecture, pathways, openings and major environmental shapes;
- negative space and panel readability.

SCENE CONTENT:
Ultra-wide night exterior seen from a low, level viewpoint across rough blue-black ground. The foreground is a shallow band of uneven earth, low scrub and scattered rocks. In the middle distance, a small steep-roofed rural hut stands in the left third, while a lower modest building sits near center, both tiny against the landscape. Sparse tree silhouettes frame the far left and right edges. A large blocky dark stone structure or wall dominates the rightmost quarter, rising from the ground and cropping out at the top/right edge. The background is a flat distant horizon beneath a broad deep-indigo starry sky occupying about half the image. Cold moonless starlight gives faint blue edge highlights; no people or creatures are visible.

COHESIVE GAME ART DIRECTION:

Do not make it cartoon, anime, painterly, plastic, glossy, oversaturated, generic concept art or an obvious 3D render. Do not redesign the composition. The result must be immediately recognizable as the same scene at photographic realism.

IMAGE-SPECIFIC NEGATIVE/QUALITY CONSTRAINTS:
No moon, sunrise, torches, windows blazing with light, travelers, animals, castle skyline, mountains, modern fencing, or added village buildings. Keep the right-hand mass large and nearly black, the huts small and low, and the horizon flat. Preserve the quiet empty negative sky and deep focus; do not use fog or shallow depth of field to hide the structures.

Output one clean scene image with no frame or caption.

Tight centered frontal portrait of the same young light-skinned woman in a deep cobalt hood as HEAD4 block 070; calm symmetrical face, dark hair hidden, triangular hood silhouette, black background.

COHESIVE GAME ART DIRECTION:
Grounded prestige live-action Forgotten Realms fantasy; realistic late-medieval materials and construction; natural skin, cloth, leather, wood, stone and metal; practical costumes and armor; physically coherent natural or motivated magical lighting; restrained cinematic color grading; subtle atmospheric depth; rich fine detail; serious dramatic tone. Match or exceed the realism and production quality of PIC1_block_080_village.png.

Do not add text, borders, logos, interface elements, modern objects, extra characters, extra limbs or unrelated fantasy decoration. Do not make it cartoon, anime, painterly, plastic, glossy, oversaturated, generic concept art or an obvious 3D render. Do not redesign the composition. The result must be immediately recognizable as the same scene at photographic realism.

IMAGE-SPECIFIC CONSTRAINTS:
Preserve the unusually wide head-portrait panel and pure featureless black background. Do not expand to a full bust or show more torso; retain the exact head size, placement, gaze, facing, silhouette and lower-edge crop. This is a matched portrait component: keep face, hair/headwear, costume palette, materials, apparent age/build and lighting coherent with BODY6_block_070_frame_000.png. Treat pixel colors as restrained material/color cues, not neon glow. Keep all empty areas solid black; no scenery, vignette, halo, smoke, props or added decoration beyond what is explicitly present.

Output one clean scene image with no frame or caption.
